\DoxyCodeLine{4203       b(1)= -\/d(1)}

\DoxyCodeLine{4205       c(1)= \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehto__units_a99185641f2fef22fbd699ff69ee64f18}{zero}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4207       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (n > 3) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4208        c(1)= c(3)/(x(4)-\/x(2))-\/c(2)/(x(3)-\/x(1))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4209        c(n)= c(n-\/1)/(x(n)-\/x(n-\/2))-\/c(n-\/2)/(x(n-\/1)-\/x(n-\/3))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4210        c(1)= c(1)*d(1)*d(1)/(x(4)-\/x(1))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4211        c(n)= -\/c(n)*d(n-\/1)*d(n-\/1)/(x(n)-\/x(n-\/3))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4212 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END IF}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4187 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4188 \textcolor{comment}{*.....Set up tridiagonal system.........................................}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4189 \textcolor{comment}{*     b=diagonal, d=offdiagonal, c=right-\/hand side}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4190 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4191       d(1)= x(2)-\/x(1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4192       c(2)= (y(2)-\/y(1))/d(1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4193       \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k= 2,n-\/1}
\DoxyCodeLine{4194        d(k)= x(k+1)-\/x(k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4195        b(k)= two*(d(k-\/1)+d(k))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4196        c(k+1)= (y(k+1)-\/y(k))/d(k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4197        c(k)= c(k+1)-\/c(k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4198 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4199 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4200 \textcolor{comment}{*.....End conditions.  third derivatives at x(1) and x(n) obtained}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4201 \textcolor{comment}{*     from divided differences.......................................}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4202 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4203       b(1)= -\/d(1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4204       b(n)= -\/d(n-\/1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4205       c(1)= \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehto__units_a99185641f2fef22fbd699ff69ee64f18}{zero}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4206       c(n)= \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacehto__units_a99185641f2fef22fbd699ff69ee64f18}{zero}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4207       \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} (n > 3) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4208        c(1)= c(3)/(x(4)-\/x(2))-\/c(2)/(x(3)-\/x(1))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4209        c(n)= c(n-\/1)/(x(n)-\/x(n-\/2))-\/c(n-\/2)/(x(n-\/1)-\/x(n-\/3))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4210        c(1)= c(1)*d(1)*d(1)/(x(4)-\/x(1))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4211        c(n)= -\/c(n)*d(n-\/1)*d(n-\/1)/(x(n)-\/x(n-\/3))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4212 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END IF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4213 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4214       \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=2,n    \textcolor{comment}{! forward elimination}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4215        t= d(k-\/1)/b(k-\/1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4216        b(k)= b(k)-\/t*d(k-\/1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4217        c(k)= c(k)-\/t*c(k-\/1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4218 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4219 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4220       c(n)= c(n)/b(n)   }
\DoxyCodeLine{4221 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4222 \textcolor{comment}{* back substitution ( makes c the sigma of text)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4223 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4224       \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=n-\/1,1,-\/1}
\DoxyCodeLine{4225        c(k)= (c(k)-\/d(k)*c(k+1))/b(k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4226 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4227 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4228 \textcolor{comment}{*.....Compute polynomial coefficients...................................}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4229 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4230       b(n)= (y(n)-\/y(n-\/1))/d(n-\/1)+d(n-\/1)*(c(n-\/1)+c(n)+c(n))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4231       \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=1,n-\/1}
\DoxyCodeLine{4232        b(k)= (y(k+1)-\/y(k))/d(k)-\/d(k)*(c(k+1)+c(k)+c(k))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4233        d(k)= (c(k+1)-\/c(k))/d(k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4234        c(k)= three*c(k)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4235 \textcolor{keywordflow}{      END DO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4236       c(n)= three*c(n)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4237       d(n)= d(n-\/1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4238 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
